Great question, Markâ€”and this oneâ€™s all about **flow** vs **structure**.

Hereâ€™s the short version:

---

## ğŸ§± If You're Building a **Linear Scroll (Single Page Flow)**:

ğŸ‘‰ **Use a `Section Break`**

- Keeps everything on one page
- Smooth scroll from Welcome â†’ How This Works â†’ Loop 0
- Good for immersive, narrative-driven experiences (akaâ€¦ the braid)
- Lets you keep background, fonts, music, etc. consistent across everything
- Cleaner transitions, fewer reloads

âœ… Recommended **if you want people to read in sequence**  
âœ… Best if youâ€™re using anchors like `/#how-this-works`

---

## ğŸ“„ If You're Building **Discrete Pages (Multi-Page Navigation)**:

ğŸ‘‰ **Use a `Container` on a New Page**

- Separates content clearly
- Loads like a new webpage (e.g. `/how-this-works`)
- More flexibility for layout/design, but less flow
- Good if you want each Loop to feel like a sacred standalone page

âœ… Recommended **if each loop is its own destination**  
âœ… Best if using buttons like â€œStart Hereâ€ â†’ loads new view

---

## ğŸ’¥ Want it to Feel Super Smooth?

Add this to your Carrd **Site Settings > Code > Footer (before `</body>`)**:

    });
  });
</script>

## ğŸ’¡ If Youâ€™re Solo-Building and Hosting on Carrdâ€¦

## âœ… 2. Enable Smooth Scrolling in Carrd (Step-by-Step)

### ğŸ”¨ Where to Put It

1. In Carrd, open your editor  
2. Click the **gear icon** (âš™ï¸) in the top-right â†’ open **â€œSite Settingsâ€**
3. Go to the **Code** tab
4. Scroll down to the **Footer** section (not Header, not Body Start)
5. **Paste this code:**

```html
<script>
  document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
    anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
      if (target) {
        target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    });
  });
</script>
```

6. Save and **publish**

## ğŸ§­ In Carrd, â€œFooterâ€ Isnâ€™t a Settings Tab â€” Itâ€™s a Special Element

To inject your **site-wide custom code** (like smooth scrolling), hereâ€™s how to do it *for real* in Carrd:

---

## âœ… HOW TO ADD SMOOTH SCROLL SCRIPT IN CARRD

### ğŸ”¨ Step-by-Step

1. **Click `+` to Add Element**
2. Choose **â€œControlâ€**
3. In the Control Elementâ€™s settings:
   - Set **Type** â†’ `Footer Marker`

   Now everything **below this block** will be considered part of the â€œfooterâ€ zone.

4. **Right below that Footer Marker**, click `+` again â†’ select **Embed**
5. Set **Embed to Inline**
6. Paste this code into the Embed:

```html
<script>
  document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
    anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
      if (target) {
        target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    });
  });
</script>
```

7. Publish â†’ Test any scroll link or index button

## ğŸ’¡ Notes

- **The Control block is the boundary**â€”Carrd sees everything after it as the footer
- **Only 1 footer marker needed** (donâ€™t duplicate)
- The floating index button can still live inside or above thisâ€”doesnâ€™t matter

**You:**

**Assistant:**

*2025-07-22 21:04:01*

âœ… **Nope â€” it does NOT need its own container.**

Carrd lets you drop a **Control â†’ Footer Marker** and then place an **Embed (Inline)** directly beneath it **without wrapping it in a container.** In fact, **keeping it outside a container is cleaner** for this type of global script.

---

## ğŸ“¦ So, in short:

- **Control block** â†’ set to `Footer Marker` âœ…
- Directly underneath that â†’ **Embed block** (set to Inline) âœ…
- **No container required**, no styling neededâ€”just raw functionality

---

## ğŸ§  Why No Container?

- Containers are great for layout/spacing
- But script embeds (like smooth scroll or tracking pixels) **donâ€™t need visual space**
- Putting it inside a container could add unintended spacing or conflict with other layout elements
